    function loadSprite() {
        var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
        xhr.open('GET', 'https://brain.com.ua/bestatic/svg/sprite.prod.svg', true);
        xhr.send();
        xhr.onload = function() {
            if (xhr.status == 200) {
                var div = document.createElement('div');
                div.style="display:hidden";
                div.innerHTML = xhr.responseText;
                document.head.append(div);
            }
        }
    }
    loadSprite();
</script>

    window.senderCallback = function() {

        if (width > 1024) {
            SenderWidget.init({companyId: "i262197037"});

    (function(d, s, id) {
        var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0];
        js = d.createElement(s);
        js.id = id;
        js.src = "https://widget.sender.mobi/build/init.js";
        fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs, 'sender-widget');

</script>

<script async>
    window.initGoogleFeedback = function() {
        var merchantId = 115272797;

        var ratingBadgeContainer = document.getElementById('google-feedback-badge-container');
        window.gapi.load('ratingbadge', function() {
            window.gapi.ratingbadge.render(
                ratingBadgeContainer, {
                    'merchant_id': merchantId,
                    'position': 'INLINE'
                }
            );
        });

        }
    }
</script>

    <!-- Observer-->
<script async>
    function isObserverExists() {
        return 'imageObserver' in window;
    }

    function initObserver() {
        if (isObserverExists() || !('IntersectionObserver' in window)) {
            return;
        }

        var options = {
            threshold: 0.3,
            rootMargin: '0px 100px 200px 100px'
        };

        window.imageObserver = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
            entries.forEach(function(entry) {
                if (entry.intersectionRatio > 0) {
                    var element = entry.target;
                    var src = element.dataset.observeSrc;

                    element.src = src;
                    window.imageObserver.unobserve(entry.target);
                }
            });
        }, options);
    }

    function observeImage(image) {
        if (isObserverExists()) {
            window.imageObserver.observe(image);
        } else {
            var src = image.dataset.observeSrc;
            image.src = src;
        }
    }

    function seekForObservableImages(element) {
        var isElement = element instanceof Element;
        var isDocument = element instanceof HTMLDocument;
        if (!isElement && !isDocument) {
            return;
        }

        var imagesSelector = 'img[data-observe-src]:not([src])';
        if (isElement && element.matches(imagesSelector)) {
            observeImage(element);
            return;
        }

        var images = Array.from(element.querySelectorAll(imagesSelector));
        if (!images || !images.length) {
            return;
        }

        images.forEach(function(image) {
            observeImage(image);
        });
    }

    initObserver();
    seekForObservableImages(document);

    document.addEventListener('DOMNodeInserted', function(e) {
        seekForObservableImages(e.target);
    });

</script>
<!-- End Observer-->

        }
